  {},\\n50: \\t\\tgvk.AuthorizationPolicy:   {},\\n51: \\t\\tgvk.RequestAuthentication: {},\\n52: \\t}\\n53: )\\n54: \\n55: // SidecarScope is a wrapper over the Sidecar resource with some\\n56: // preprocessed data to determine the list of services, virtualServices,\\n57: // and destinationRules that are accessible to a given\\n58: // sidecar. Precomputing the list of services, virtual services, dest rules\\n59: // for a sidecar improves performance as we no longer need to compute this\\n60: // list for every sidecar. We simply have to match a sidecar to a\\n61: // SidecarScope. Note that this is not the same as public/private scoped\\n62: // services. The list of services seen by every sidecar scope (namespace\\n63: // wide or per workload) depends on the imports, the listeners, and other\\n64: // settings.\\n65: //\\n66: // Every proxy workload of SidecarProxy type will always map to a\\n67: // SidecarScope object. If the proxy's namespace does not have a user\\n68: // specified Sidecar CRD, we will construct one that has a catch all egress\\n69: // listener that imports every public service/virtualService in the mesh.\\n70: type SidecarScope struct {\\n71: \\tName string\\n72: \\t// This is the namespace where the sidecar takes effect,\\n73: \\t// maybe different from the ns where sidecar resides if sidecar is in root ns.\\n74: \\tNamespace string\\n75: \\t// The crd itself. A sidecar\\n83: \\t// scope should have either ingress/egress listeners or both.  For\\n84: \\t// every proxy workload that maps to a sidecar API object (or the\\n85: \\t// default object), we will go through every egress listener in the\\n86: \\t// object and process the Envoy listener or RDS based on the imported\\n87: \\t// services/virtual services in that listener.\\n88: \\tEgressListeners []*IstioEgressListenerWrapper\\n89: \\n90: \\t// Union of services imported across all egress listeners for use by CDS code.\\n91: \\tservices           []*Service\\n92: \\tservicesByHostname map[host.Name]*Service\\n93: \\n94: \\t// Destination rules imported across all egress listeners. Each hostname in this map\\n98: \\t// corresponds to a service in the services array above. is a wrapper over the Sidecar resource with some\n56: // preprocessed data to determine the list of services, virtualServices,\n57: // and destinationRules that are accessible to a given\n58: // sidecar. Precomputing the list of services, virtual services, dest rules\n59: // for a sidecar improves performance as we no longer need to compute this\n60: // list for every sidecar. We simply have to match a sidecar to a\n61: // SidecarScope. Note that this is not the same as public/private scoped\n62: // services. The list of services seen by every sidecar scope (namespace\n63: // wide or per workload) depends on the imports, the listeners, and other\n64: // settings.\n65: //\n66: // Every proxy workload of SidecarProxy type will always map to a\n67: // SidecarScope object. Each hostname in this map\n98: \t// corresponds to a service in the services array above. \treturn out\n251: }\n252: \n253: // ConvertToSidecarScope converts from Sidecar config to SidecarScope object\n254: func ConvertToSidecarScope(ps *PushContext, sidecarConfig *config.Config, Each registry is responsible for tracking a set\n261: // of endpoints associated with mesh services, and calling the EDSUpdate on changes.\n262: // A registry may group endpoints for a service in smaller subsets - for example by\n263: // deployment, or to deal with very large number of endpoints for a service. We want\n264: // to avoid passing around large objects - like full list of endpoints for a registry,\n265: // or the full list of endpoints for a service across registries, since it limits\n266: // scalability.\n267: //\n268: // Future optimizations will include grouping the endpoints by labels, gateway or region to\n269: // reduce the time when subsetting or split-horizon is used. \n327: // PushRequest defines a request to push to proxies\n328: // It is used to send updates to the config update debouncer and pass to the PushQueue.\n329: type PushRequest struct {\n330: \t// Full determines whether a full push is required or not. If false, an incremental update will be sent.\n331: \t// Incremental pushes:\n332: \t// * Do not recompute the push context\n333: \t// * Do not recompute proxy state (such as ServiceInstances)\n334: \t// * Are not reported in standard metrics such as push time\n335: \t// As a result, configuration updates should never be incremental. Generally, only EDS will set this, but\n336: \t// in the future SDS will as well.\n337: \tFull bool\n338: \n339: \t// ConfigsUpdated keeps track of configs that have changed.\n340: \t// This is used as an optimization to avoid unnecessary pushes to proxies that are scoped with a Sidecar.\n341: \t// If this is empty, then all proxies will get an update.\n342: \t// Otherwise only proxies depend on these configs will get an update.\n343: \t// The kind of resources are defined in pkg/config/schemas.\n344: \tConfigsUpdated map[ConfigKey]struct{}\n345: \n346: \t// Push stores the push context to use for the update. This may initially be nil, as we will\n347: \t// debounce changes before a PushContext is eventually created.\n348: \tPush *PushContext\n349: \n350: \t// Start represents the time a push was started. This represents the time of adding to the PushQueue.\n351: \t// Note that this does not include time spent debouncing.\n352: \tStart time.Time\n353: \n354: \t// Reason represents the reason for requesting a push. This should only be a fixed set of values,\n355: \t// to avoid unbounded cardinality in metrics. If this is not set, it may be automatically filled in later.\n356: \t// There should only be multiple reasons if the push request is the result of two distinct triggers, rather than\n357: \t// classifying a single trigger as having multiple reasons.\n358: \tReason []TriggerReason\n359: \n360: \t// Delta defines the resources that were added or removed as part of this push request.\n361: \t// This is set only on requests from the client which change the set of resources they (un)subscribe from.\n362: \tDelta ResourceDelta\n363: }\n364: \n365: // ResourceDelta records the difference in requested resources by an XDS client\n366: type ResourceDelta struct {\n367: \t// Subscribed indicates the client requested these additional resources\n368: \tSubscribed sets.Set\n369: \t// && len(rd.Unsubscribed) == 0\n375: }\n376: \n377: type TriggerReason string\n378: \n379: // If adding a new reason, update xds/monitoring.go:triggerMetric\n380: const (\n381: \t// EndpointUpdate \tNamespaceUpdate TriggerReason = \"namespace\"\n403: \t// ClusterUpdate describes a push triggered by a Cluster change\n404: \tClusterUpdate TriggerReason = \"cluster\"\n405: )\n406: \n407: // Merge two update requests together\n408: // Merge behaves similarly to a list append; usage should in the form `a = a.merge(b)`.\n409: // Importantly, Merge may decide to allocate a new PushRequest object or reuse the existing one - both\n410: // inputs should not be used after completion.\n411: func (pr *PushRequest) Merge(other *PushRequest) *PushRequest {\n412: \tif pr == nil {\n413: \t\treturn other\n414: \t}\n415: \tif other == nil {\n416: \t\treturn pr\n417: \t}\n418: \n419: \t// Keep the first (older) start time\n420: \n421: \t// Merge the two reasons. Note that we shouldn't deduplicate here, or we would under count\n422: \tpr.Reason = append(pr.Reason, other.Reason...)\n423: \n424: \t// If either is full we need a full push\n425: \tpr.Full = pr.Full || other.Full\n426: \n427: \t// The other push context is presumed to be later and more up to date\n428: \tif other.Push != nil {\n429: \t\tpr.Push = other.Push\n430: \t}\n431: \n432: \t// Do not merge when any one is empty\n433: \tif len(pr.ConfigsUpdated) == 0 || len(other.ConfigsUpdated) == 0 {\n434: \t\tpr.ConfigsUpdated = nil\n435: \t} else {\n436: \t\tfor conf := range other.ConfigsUpdated {\n437: \t\t\tpr.ConfigsUpdated[conf] = struct{}{}\n438: \t\t}\n439: \t}\n440: \n441: \treturn pr\n442: }\n443: \n444: // CopyMerge two update requests together. Unlike Merge, this will not mutate either input.\n445: // This should be used when we are modifying a shared PushRequest (typically any time it's in the context\n446: // of a single proxy)\n447: func (pr *PushRequest) CopyMerge(other *PushRequest) *PushRequest {\n448: \tif pr == nil {\n449: \t\treturn other\n450: \t}\n451: \tif other == nil {\n452: \t\treturn pr\n453: \t}\n454: \n455: \tvar reason []TriggerReason\n456: \tif len(pr.Reason)+len(other.Reason) > 0 {\n457: \t\treason = make([]TriggerReason, 0, len(pr.Reason)+len(other.Reason))\n458: \t\treason = append(reason, pr.Reason...)\n459: \t\treason = append(reason, other.Reason...)\n460: \t}\n461: \tmerged := &PushRequest{\n462: \t\t// Keep the first (older) start time\n463: \t\tStart: pr.Start,\n464: \n465: \t\t// If either is full we need a full push\n466: \t\tFull: pr.Full || other.Full,\n467: \n468: \t\t// The other push context is presumed to be later and more up to date\n469: \t\tPush: other.Push,\n470: \n471: \t\t// Merge the two reasons. Note that we shouldn't deduplicate here, or we would under count\n472: \t\tReason: reason,\n473: \t}\n474: \n475: \t// Do not merge when any one is empty\n476: \tif len(pr.ConfigsUpdated) > 0 && len(other.ConfigsUpdated) > 0 {\n477: \t\tmerged.ConfigsUpdated = make(map[ConfigKey]struct{}, len(pr.ConfigsUpdated)+len(other.ConfigsUpdated))\n478: \t\tfor conf := range pr.ConfigsUpdated {\n479: \t\t\tmerged.ConfigsUpdated[conf] = struct{}{}\n480: \t\t}\n481: \t\tfor conf := range other.ConfigsUpdated {\n482: \t\t\tmerged.ConfigsUpdated[conf] = struct{}{}\n483: \t\t}\n484: \t}\n485: \n486: \treturn merged\n487: }\n488: \n489: func (pr *PushRequest) PushReason() string {\n490: \tif len(pr.Reason) == 1 && pr.Reason[0] == ProxyRequest {\n491: \t\treturn \" request\"\n492: \t}\n493: \treturn \"\"\n494: }\n495: \n496: // ProxyPushStatus represents an event captured during config push to proxies.\n497: // It may contain additional message and the affected proxy.\n498: type ProxyPushStatus struct {\n499: \tProxy   string `json:\"proxy,omitempty\"`\n500: \tMessage string `json:\"message,omitempty\"`\n501: }\n502: \n503: // AddMetric will add an case to the metric.\n504: func (ps *PushContext) AddMetric(metric monitoring.Metric, key string, proxyID, msg string) {\n505: \tif ps == nil {\n506: \t\tlog.Infof(\"Metric without context %s %v %s\", key, proxyID, msg)\n507: \t\treturn\n508: \t}\n509: \tps.proxyStatusMutex.Lock()\n510: \tdefer ps.proxyStatusMutex.Unlock()\n511: \n512: \tmetricMap, f := ps.ProxyStatus[metric.Name()]\n513: \tif !f {\n514: \t\tmetricMap = map[string]ProxyPushStatus{}\n515: \t\tps.ProxyStatus[metric.Name()] = metricMap\n516: \t}\n517: \tev := ProxyPushStatus{Message: msg, Proxy: proxyID}\n518: \tmetricMap[key] = ev\n519: }\n520: \n521: var (\n522: \n523: \t// EndpointNoPod tracks endpoints without an associated pod. The SidecarScope object is a semi-processed view of the service\n907: // registry, and config state associated with the sidecar crd. The scope contains\n908: // a set of inbound and outbound listeners, services/configs per listener,\n909: // etc. The sidecar scopes are precomputed in the initSidecarContext\n910: // function based on the Sidecar API objects in each namespace. If there is\n911: // no sidecar api object, a default sidecarscope is assigned to the\n912: // namespace which enables connectivity to all services in the mesh.\n913: //\n914: // Callers can check if the sidecarScope is from user generated object or not\n915: // by checking the sidecarScope.Config field, that contains the user provided config\n916: func (ps *PushContext) getSidecarScope(proxy *Proxy, workloadLabels labels.Collection) *SidecarScope {\n917: \t// Find the most specific matching sidecar config from the proxy's\n918: \t// config namespace If none found, construct a sidecarConfig on the fly\n919: \t// that allows the sidecar to talk to any namespace (the default\n920: \t// behavior in the absence of sidecars).\n921: \tif sidecars, ok := ps.sidecarIndex.sidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace]; ok {\n922: \t\t// TODO: logic to merge multiple sidecar resources\n923: \t\t// Currently we assume that there will be only one sidecar config for a namespace.\n924: \t\tif proxy.Type == Router {\n925: \t\t\tfor _, wrapper := range sidecars {\n926: \t\t\t\t// Gateways should just have a default scope with egress: */*\n927: \t\t\t\tif wrapper.Sidecar == nil {\n928: \t\t\t\t\treturn wrapper\n929: \t\t\t\t}\n930: \t\t\t}\n931: \t\t}\n932: \t\tif proxy.Type == SidecarProxy {\n933: \t\t\tfor _, wrapper := range sidecars {\n934: \t\t\t\tif wrapper.Sidecar != nil {\n935: \t\t\t\t\tsidecar := wrapper.Sidecar\n936: \t\t\t\t\t// if there is no workload selector, the config applies to all workloads\n937: \t\t\t\t\t// if there is a workload selector, check for matching workload labels\n938: \t\t\t\t\tif sidecar.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil {\n939: \t\t\t\t\t\tworkloadSelector := labels.Instance(sidecar.GetWorkloadSelector().GetLabels())\n940: \t\t\t\t\t\t// exclude workload selector that not match\n941: \t\t\t\t\t\tif !workloadLabels.IsSupersetOf(workloadSelector) {\n942: \t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n943: \t\t\t\t\t\t}\n944: \t\t\t\t\t}\n945: \n946: \t\t\t\t\t// it is guaranteed sidecars with selectors are put in front\n947: \t\t\t\t\t// and the sidecars are sorted by creation timestamp,\n948: \t\t\t\t\t// return exact/wildcard matching one directly\n949: \t\t\t\t\treturn wrapper\n950: \t\t\t\t}\n951: \t\t\t\t// this happens at last, it is the default sidecar scope\n952: \t\t\t\treturn wrapper\n953: \t\t\t}\n954: \t\t}\n955: \t}\n956: \n957: \t// We didn't have a Sidecar in the namespace. This means we should use the default - either an implicit\n958: \t// default selecting everything, or pulling from the root namespace.\n959: \tps.sidecarIndex.defaultSidecarMu.Lock()\n960: \tdefer ps.sidecarIndex.defaultSidecarMu.Unlock()\n961: \tif proxy.Type == Router {\n962: \t\tsc, f := ps.sidecarIndex.gatewayDefaultSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace]\n963: \t\tif f {\n964: \t\t\t// We have already computed the scope for this namespace, just fetch it\n965: \t\t\treturn sc\n966: \t\t}\n967: \t\tcomputed := DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps, proxy.ConfigNamespace)\n968: \t\tps.sidecarIndex.gatewayDefaultSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace] = computed\n969: \t\treturn computed\n970: \t}\n971: \tsc, f := ps.sidecarIndex.computedSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace]\n972: \tif f {\n973: \t\t// We have already computed the scope for this namespace, just fetch it\n974: \t\treturn sc\n975: \t}\n976: \t// We need to compute this namespace\n977: \tvar computed *SidecarScope\n978: \tif ps.sidecarIndex.rootConfig != nil {\n979: \t\tcomputed = ConvertToSidecarScope(ps, ps.sidecarIndex.rootConfig, proxy.ConfigNamespace)\n980: \t} else {\n981: \t\tcomputed = DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps, proxy.ConfigNamespace)\n982: \t\t// Even though we are a sidecar, we can store this as a gateway one since it could be used by a gateway\n983: \t\tps.sidecarIndex.gatewayDefaultSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace] = computed\n984: \t}\n985: \tps.sidecarIndex.computedSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace] = computed\n986: \treturn computed\n987: }\n988: \n989: // destinationRule returns a destination rule for a service name in a given namespace.\n990: func (ps *PushContext) destinationRule(proxyNameSpace string, service *Service) []*config.Config {\n991: \tif service == nil {\n992: \t\treturn nil\n993: \t}\n994: \t// If the proxy config namespace is same as the root config namespace\n995: \t// look for dest rules in the service's namespace first. This hack is needed\n996: \t// because sometimes, istio-system tends to become the root config namespace.\n997: \t// Destination rules are defined here for global purposes. We do not want these\n998: \t// catch all destination rules to be the only dest rule, when processing CDS for\n999: \t// proxies like the istio-ingressgateway or istio-egressgateway.\n1000: \t// If there are no service specific dest rules, we will end up picking up the same\n1001: \t// rules anyway, later in the code\n1002: \n1003: \t// 1. select destination rule from proxy config namespace\n1004: \tif proxyNameSpace != ps.Mesh.RootNamespace {\n1005: \t\t// search through the DestinationRules in proxy's namespace first\n1006: \t\tif ps.destinationRuleIndex.namespaceLocal[proxyNameSpace] != nil {\n1007: \t\t\tif hostname, ok := MostSpecificHostMatch(service.Hostname,\n1008: \t\t\t\tps.destinationRuleIndex.namespaceLocal[proxyNameSpace].destRules,\n1009: \t\t\t); ok {\n1010: \t\t\t\treturn ps.destinationRuleIndex.namespaceLocal[proxyNameSpace].destRules[hostname]\n1011: \t\t\t}\n1012: \t\t}\n1013: \t} else {\n1014: \t\t// If this is a namespace local DR in the same namespace, this must be meant for this proxy, so we do not\n1015: \t\t// need to worry about overriding other DRs with *.local type rules here. If we ignore this, then exportTo=. in\n1016: \t\t// root namespace would always be ignored\n1017: \t\tif hostname, ok := MostSpecificHostMatch(service.Hostname,\n1018: \t\t\tps.destinationRuleIndex.rootNamespaceLocal.destRules,\n1019: \t\t); ok {\n1020: \t\t\treturn ps.destinationRuleIndex.rootNamespaceLocal.destRules[hostname]\n1021: \t\t}\n1022: \t}\n1023: \n1024: \t// 2. select destination rule from service namespace\n1025: \tsvcNs := service.Attributes.Namespace\n1026: \n1027: \t// This can happen when finding the subset labels for a proxy in root namespace.\n1028: \t// Because based on a pure cluster's fqdn, we do not know the service and\n1029: \t// construct a fake service without setting Attributes at all.\n1030: \tif svcNs == \"\" {\n1031: \t\tfor _, svc := range ps.servicesExportedToNamespace(proxyNameSpace) {\n1032: \t\t\tif service.Hostname == svc.Hostname && svc.Attributes.Namespace != \"\" {\n1033: \t\t\t\tsvcNs = svc.Attributes.Namespace\n1034: \t\t\t\tbreak\n1035: \t\t\t}\n1036: \t\t}\n1037: \t}\n1038: \n1039: \t// 3. if no private/public rule matched in the calling proxy's namespace,\n1040: \t// check the target service's namespace for exported rules\n1041: \tif svcNs != \"\" {\n1042: \t\tif out := ps.getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace(svcNs, service.Hostname, proxyNameSpace); out != nil {\n1043: \t\t\treturn out\n1044: \t\t}\n1045: \t}\n1046: \n1047: \t// 4. if no public/private rule in calling proxy's namespace matched, and no public rule in the\n1048: \t// target service's namespace matched, search for any exported destination rule in the config root namespace\n1049: \tif out := ps.getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace(ps.Mesh.RootNamespace, service.Hostname, proxyNameSpace); out != nil {\n1050: \t\treturn out\n1051: \t}\n1052: \n1053: \t// 5. service DestinationRules were merged in SetDestinationRules, return mesh/namespace rules if present\n1054: \tif features.EnableDestinationRuleInheritance {\n1055: \t\t// return namespace rule if present\n1056: \t\tif out := ps.destinationRuleIndex.inheritedByNamespace[proxyNameSpace]; out != nil {\n1057: \t\t\treturn []*config.Config{out}\n1058: \t\t}\n1059: \t\t// return mesh rule\n1060: \t\tif out := ps.destinationRuleIndex.inheritedByNamespace[ps.Mesh.RootNamespace]; out != nil {\n1061: \t\t\treturn []*config.Config{out}\n1062: \t\t}\n1063: \t}\n1064: \n1065: \treturn nil\n1066: }\n1067: \n1068: func (ps *PushContext) getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace(owningNamespace string, hostname host.Name, clientNamespace string) []*config.Config {\n1069: \tif ps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace] != nil {\n1070: \t\tif specificHostname, ok := MostSpecificHostMatch(hostname,\n1071: \t\t\tps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace].destRules,\n1072: \t\t); ok {\n1073: \t\t\t// Check if the dest rule for this host is actually exported to the proxy's (client) namespace\n1074: \t\t\texportToMap := ps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace].exportTo[specificHostname]\n1075: \t\t\tif len(exportToMap) == 0 || exportToMap[visibility.Public] || exportToMap[visibility.Instance(clientNamespace)] {\n1076: \t\t\t\tif features.EnableDestinationRuleInheritance {\n1077: \t\t\t\t\tvar parent *config.Config\n1078: nil\n1100: }\n1101: \n1102: // IsClusterLocal indicates whether the endpoints for the service should only be accessible to clients\n1103: // within the cluster.\n1104: func (ps *PushContext) *PushContext) InitContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest) error {\n1115: \t// Acquire a lock to ensure we don't concurrently initialize the same nil\n1346: }\n1347: \n1348: // Caches list of services in the registry, and creates a map\n1349: // of hostname to service\n1350: func (ps *PushContext) initServiceRegistry(env *Environment) error {\n1351: \t// Sort the services in order of creation.\n1352: \tallServices := SortServicesByCreationTime(env.Services())\n1353: \tfor _, s := range allServices {\n1354: \t\tsvcKey := s.Key()\n1355: \t\t// Precache instances\n1356: \t\tfor _, port := range s.Ports {\n1357: \t\t\tif _, ok := ps.ServiceIndex.instancesByPort[svcKey]; !ok {\n1358: \t\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.instancesByPort[svcKey] = make(map[int][]*ServiceInstance)\n1359: \t\t\t}\n1360: \t\t\tinstances := make([]*ServiceInstance, 0)\n1361: \t\t\tinstances = append(instances, env.InstancesByPort(s, port.Port, nil)...)\n1362: \t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.instancesByPort[svcKey][port.Port] = instances\n1363: \t\t}\n1364: \n1365: \t\tif _, f := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[s.Hostname]; !f {\n1366: \t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[s.Hostname] = map[string]*Service{}\n1367: \t\t}\n1368: \t\tps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[s.Hostname][s.Attributes.Namespace] = s\n1369: \n1370: = append(ps.ServiceIndex.privateByNamespace[ns], s)\n1374: \t\t\t} else if ps.exportToDefaults.service[visibility.Public] {\n1375: \t\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.public = append(ps.ServiceIndex.public, s)\n1376: \t\t\t}\n1377: \t\t} else {\n1378: \t\t\t// if service has exportTo ~ - i.e. not visible to anyone, ignore all exportTos\n1379: \t\t\t// if service has exportTo *, make public and ignore all other exportTos\n1380: \t\t\t// if service has exportTo ., replace with current namespace\n1381: \t\t\tif s.Attributes.ExportTo[visibility.Public] {\n1382: \t\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.public = append(ps.ServiceIndex.public, s)\n1383: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n1384: \t\t\t} else if s.Attributes.ExportTo[visibility.None] {\n1385: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n1386: \t\t\t} else {\n1387: \t\t\t\t// . or other namespaces\n1388: \t\t\t\tfor exportTo := range s.Attributes.ExportTo {\n1389: \t\t\t\t\tif exportTo == visibility.Private || string(exportTo) == ns {\n1390: \t\t\t\t\t\t// exportTo with same bool {\n1409: \t\t// If creation time is the same, then behavior is nondeterministic. uncommon.\n1412: \t\tif services[i].CreationTime.Equal(services[j].CreationTime) {\n1413: \t\t\tin := services[i].Attributes.Name + \".\" + services[i].Attributes.Namespace\n1414: \t\t\tjn := \t})\n1419: \treturn services\n1420: }\n1421: \n1422: // Caches list of service accounts in the registry\n1423: func (ps *PushContext) initServiceAccounts(env *Environment, services []*Service) {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01AozkPfwPUfkCG25cEbpmPp","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01SBj5wuZkhQgWptyDdRKzEe","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/logs/agent/investigation.md","content":"# Investigation Report: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update\n\n## Summary\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules (DRs) target the same host, Istio merges them into a single consolidated configuration during PushContext initialization. The merging process **loses the metadata identity (Name/Namespace) of contributing DRs**, causing only one DR's ConfigKey to be registered in the SidecarScope's config dependencies. When a non-primary DR is updated, the xDS push filter uses DependsOnConfig() to check if the proxy is affected, but the check fails because the updated DR's ConfigKey was never registered. As a result, the xDS push is **silently skipped**, and the Envoy sidecar receives no updated configuration until the pod is restarted.\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause is the **loss of metadata identity during DestinationRule merging**, combined with **incomplete dependency tracking** and **incorrect xDS push filtering**.\n\n### Mechanism\n\n1. **Metadata Loss During Merge** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n   - The `mergeDestinationRule()` function merges multiple DRs for the same host by:\n     - Finding the existing DR in `p.destRules[hostname]`\n     - Modifying the EXISTING DR's config object in-place (subsets, traffic policies)\n     - If selectors match, setting `addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false` (line 60)\n     - NOT appending the new DR's config to the list (line 102 is skipped when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules == false`)\n   - **Result**: Only the first DR's `config.Config` object survives in `p.destRules[hostname]`. The second (and subsequent) DR's Name/Namespace metadata is **never stored**.\n\n2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:219-227`)\n   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` iterates over `ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s)` results\n   - For each returned DR, it calls:\n     ```go\n     out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n         Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n         Name:      dr.Name,      // Only the MERGED DR's name\n         Namespace: dr.Namespace, // Only the MERGED DR's namespace\n     })\n     ```\n   - Since `ps.destinationRule()` returns only one `config.Config` per hostname (the merged one), only ONE ConfigKey is registered.\n   - **Result**: The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `sc.configDependencies`.\n\n3. **Push Filter Skips Unknown ConfigKeys** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:521-540`)\n   - When a config update occurs, `DependsOnConfig()` checks if the proxy depends on that config:\n     ```go\n     _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n     return exists\n     ```\n   - The HashCode is based on Kind, Name, and Namespace (lines 60-74 in `pilot/pkg/model/config.go`)\n   - If the updated DR's ConfigKey hash is NOT in the map, `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`.\n\n4. **xDS Push Is Skipped** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go:60-74` and `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:688`)\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` calls `proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config)` (line 64)\n   - If it returns `false`, the push is filtered out\n   - At line 688 of `ads.go`, if `ProxyNeedsPush()` returns `false`, the push to the proxy is **skipped entirely**\n   - The proxy receives no updated xDS configuration and continues serving stale routes/clusters\n\n---\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1. Merge Function Loses Metadata (`destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n\n**Line 38-60: Merge Detection and Decision**\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, ...) {\n    rule := destRuleConfig.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    resolvedHost := ResolveShortnameToFQDN(rule.Host, destRuleConfig.Meta)\n    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n        addRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n        for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n            existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            bothWithoutSelector := rule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil && existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil\n            bothWithSelector := existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil\n            selectorsMatch := labels.Instance(existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels()).Equals(rule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n\n            if bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n                addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false  // LINE 60: Don't add new DR\n            }\n```\n\n**Lines 63-93: Merge Data Into Existing Config**\n```go\n            copied := mdr.DeepCopy()  // Deep copy the EXISTING config\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n            mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\n            // Add subsets from new rule to existing rule\n            for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n                if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                    mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Add traffic policy if missing\n            if mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n                mergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n            }\n        }\n```\n\n**Lines 101-104: New DR Config Is NOT Added**\n```go\n        if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {  // This is FALSE when merged\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n        }\n        return  // Exit without adding new DR's config\n    }\n```\n\n**Result**: The second DR's `config.Config` object (with Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\") is never stored.\n\n---\n\n### 2. Incomplete Dependency Registration (`sidecar.go:219-227`)\n\n**DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace() registers only merged DRs:**\n```go\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,         // Only MERGED DR's name\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,    // Only MERGED DR's namespace\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\nSince `out.destinationRules` is populated from `ps.destinationRule()` (line 209), which returns only the merged config, only one DR's metadata is registered.\n\nSimilarly, lines 410-416 in `ConvertToSidecarScope()`:\n```go\nfor _, dr := range drList {\n    out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n        Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n        Name:      dr.Name,      // Only MERGED DR\n        Namespace: dr.Namespace,\n    })\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. ConfigKey Hash Lookup (`config.go:60-74` and `sidecar.go:538`)\n\n**ConfigKey.HashCode() is based on Name, Namespace, and Kind:**\n```go\nfunc (key ConfigKey) HashCode() uint64 {\n    hash := md5.New()\n    for _, v := range []string{\n        key.Name,       // Different for \"reviews-subsets\" vs \"reviews-traffic-policy\"\n        key.Namespace,  // Same\n        key.Kind.Kind,  // Same (DestinationRule)\n        key.Kind.Group,\n        key.Kind.Version,\n    } {\n        hash.Write([]byte(v))\n    }\n    ...\n    return binary.BigEndian.Uint64(sum)\n}\n```\n\n**DependsOnConfig() checks for the hash:**\n```go\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) DependsOnConfig(config ConfigKey) bool {\n    if sc == nil {\n        return true\n    }\n    ...\n    _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n    return exists  // FALSE if \"reviews-subsets\" was never registered\n}\n```\n\nWhen `reviews-subsets` is updated, DependsOnConfig() is called with:\n```\nConfigKey{Kind: DestinationRule, Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\"}\n```\n\nIts hash is NOT in `configDependencies` because only \"reviews-traffic-policy\" was registered.\n\n---\n\n### 4. xDS Push Filtering (`proxy_dependencies.go:60-74` and `ads.go:688`)\n\n**checkProxyDependencies() calls DependsOnConfig():**\n```go\nfunc checkProxyDependencies(proxy *model.Proxy, config model.ConfigKey) bool {\n    switch proxy.Type {\n    case model.SidecarProxy:\n        if proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {  // Returns FALSE\n            return true\n        } else if proxy.PrevSidecarScope != nil && proxy.PrevSidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false  // Returns FALSE here\n}\n```\n\n**ConfigAffectsProxy() uses checkProxyDependencies():**\n```go\nfunc ConfigAffectsProxy(req *model.PushRequest, proxy *model.Proxy) bool {\n    for config := range req.ConfigsUpdated {\n        if affected && checkProxyDependencies(proxy, config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false  // Returns FALSE\n}\n```\n\n**DefaultProxyNeedsPush() checks ConfigAffectsProxy():**\n```go\nfunc DefaultProxyNeedsPush(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) bool {\n    if ConfigAffectsProxy(req, proxy) {  // Returns FALSE\n        return true\n    }\n    ...\n    return false  // Returns FALSE\n}\n```\n\n**ads.go:688 skips the push:**\n```go\nif !s.ProxyNeedsPush(con.proxy, pushRequest) {\n    log.Debugf(\"Skipping push to %v, no updates required\", con.conID)\n    if pushRequest.Full {\n        reportAllEvents(s.StatusReporter, con.conID, pushRequest.Push.LedgerVersion, nil)\n    }\n    return nil  // PUSH IS SKIPPED\n}\n```\n\nThe proxy receives no updated configuration and continues serving stale Envoy routes and clusters.\n\n---\n\n### 5. Consolidated Structure Hides Multiple DRs (`push_context.go:251-256`)\n\n```go\ntype consolidatedDestRules struct {\n    exportTo map[host.Name]map[visibility.Instance]bool\n    destRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config  // Map of hostname to LIST of configs\n}\n```\n\nWhile the structure supports multiple DRs per hostname (a list), the merging process ensures that:\n- For matching selectors, only ONE config object survives\n- The others' metadata is lost, making them \"invisible\" to dependency tracking\n\n---\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`** - Merges multiple DRs, loses metadata\n2. **`pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`** - Stores merged DRs in index, no tracking of contributing DRs\n3. **`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`** - Registers only merged DR's metadata in configDependencies\n4. **`pilot/pkg/model/config.go`** - ConfigKey hash depends on Name/Namespace\n5. **`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go`** - Filters pushes using DependsOnConfig() check\n6. **`pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`** - Skips push if ProxyNeedsPush() returns false\n7. **`pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go`** - Similar push filtering for incremental updates\n\n---\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n```\nStep 1: Multiple DestinationRules for same host are created\n        |\n        v\nStep 2: mergeDestinationRule() merges DR-2 into DR-1\n        - Modifies DR-1's config object in-place\n        - Sets addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false\n        - Does NOT add DR-2's config.Config to destRules[hostname] list\n        |\n        v\nStep 3: Only DR-1's metadata (Name, Namespace) is stored\n        - DR-2's metadata is completely lost\n        - p.destRules[hostname] = [DR-1 config only]\n        |\n        v\nStep 4: DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace() registers config dependencies\n        - Iterates over ps.destinationRule() results\n        - {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01SBj5wuZkhQgWptyDdRKzEe","type":"tool_result","content":"File created successfully at: /logs/agent/investigation.md"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a0677410-f91b-4a17-82cc-b277098bad2c","uuid":"d590f94c-80c3-4cae-b6f3-b5639fddb058","tool_use_result":{"type":"create","filePath":"/logs/agent/investigation.md","content":"# Investigation Report: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update\n\n## Summary\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules (DRs) target the same host, Istio merges them into a single consolidated configuration during PushContext initialization. The merging process **loses the metadata identity (Name/Namespace) of contributing DRs**, causing only one DR's ConfigKey to be registered in the SidecarScope's config dependencies. When a non-primary DR is updated, the xDS push filter uses DependsOnConfig() to check if the proxy is affected, but the check fails because the updated DR's ConfigKey was never registered. As a result, the xDS push is **silently skipped**, and the Envoy sidecar receives no updated configuration until the pod is restarted.\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause is the **loss of metadata identity during DestinationRule merging**, combined with **incomplete dependency tracking** and **incorrect xDS push filtering**.\n\n### Mechanism\n\n1. **Metadata Loss During Merge** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n   - The `mergeDestinationRule()` function merges multiple DRs for the same host by:\n     - Finding the existing DR in `p.destRules[hostname]`\n     - Modifying the EXISTING DR's config object in-place (subsets, traffic policies)\n     - If selectors match, setting `addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false` (line 60)\n     - NOT appending the new DR's config to the list (line 102 is skipped when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules == false`)\n   - **Result**: Only the first DR's `config.Config` object survives in `p.destRules[hostname]`. The second (and subsequent) DR's Name/Namespace metadata is **never stored**.\n\n2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:219-227`)\n   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` iterates over `ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s)` results\n   - For each returned DR, it calls:\n     ```go\n     out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n         Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n         Name:      dr.Name,      // Only the MERGED DR's name\n         Namespace: dr.Namespace, // Only the MERGED DR's namespace\n     })\n     ```\n   - Since `ps.destinationRule()` returns only one `config.Config` per hostname (the merged one), only ONE ConfigKey is registered.\n   - **Result**: The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `sc.configDependencies`.\n\n3. **Push Filter Skips Unknown ConfigKeys** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:521-540`)\n   - When a config update occurs, `DependsOnConfig()` checks if the proxy depends on that config:\n     ```go\n     _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n     return exists\n     ```\n   - The HashCode is based on Kind, Name, and Namespace (lines 60-74 in `pilot/pkg/model/config.go`)\n   - If the updated DR's ConfigKey hash is NOT in the map, `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`.\n\n4. **xDS Push Is Skipped** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go:60-74` and `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:688`)\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` calls `proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config)` (line 64)\n   - If it returns `false`, the push is filtered out\n   - At line 688 of `ads.go`, if `ProxyNeedsPush()` returns `false`, the push to the proxy is **skipped entirely**\n   - The proxy receives no updated xDS configuration and continues serving stale routes/clusters\n\n---\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1. Merge Function Loses Metadata (`destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n\n**Line 38-60: Merge Detection and Decision**\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, ...) {\n    rule := destRuleConfig.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    resolvedHost := ResolveShortnameToFQDN(rule.Host, destRuleConfig.Meta)\n    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n        addRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n        for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n            existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            bothWithoutSelector := rule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil && existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil\n            bothWithSelector := existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil\n            selectorsMatch := labels.Instance(existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels()).Equals(rule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n\n            if bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n                addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false  // LINE 60: Don't add new DR\n            }\n```\n\n**Lines 63-93: Merge Data Into Existing Config**\n```go\n            copied := mdr.DeepCopy()  // Deep copy the EXISTING config\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n            mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\n            // Add subsets from new rule to existing rule\n            for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n                if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                    mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Add traffic policy if missing\n            if mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n                mergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n            }\n        }\n```\n\n**Lines 101-104: New DR Config Is NOT Added**\n```go\n        if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {  // This is FALSE when merged\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n        }\n        return  // Exit without adding new DR's config\n    }\n```\n\n**Result**: The second DR's `config.Config` object (with Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\") is never stored.\n\n---\n\n### 2. Incomplete Dependency Registration (`sidecar.go:219-227`)\n\n**DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace() registers only merged DRs:**\n```go\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,         // Only MERGED DR's name\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,    // Only MERGED DR's namespace\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\nSince `out.destinationRules` is populated from `ps.destinationRule()` (line 209), which returns only the merged config, only one DR's metadata is registered.\n\nSimilarly, lines 410-416 in `ConvertToSidecarScope()`:\n```go\nfor _, dr := range drList {\n    out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n        Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n        Name:      dr.Name,      // Only MERGED DR\n        Namespace: dr.Namespace,\n    })\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. ConfigKey Hash Lookup (`config.go:60-74` and `sidecar.go:538`)\n\n**ConfigKey.HashCode() is based on Name, Namespace, and Kind:**\n```go\nfunc (key ConfigKey) HashCode() uint64 {\n    hash := md5.New()\n    for _, v := range []string{\n        key.Name,       // Different for \"reviews-subsets\" vs \"reviews-traffic-policy\"\n        key.Namespace,  // Same\n        key.Kind.Kind,  // Same (DestinationRule)\n        key.Kind.Group,\n        key.Kind.Version,\n    } {\n        hash.Write([]byte(v))\n    }\n    ...\n    return binary.BigEndian.Uint64(sum)\n}\n```\n\n**DependsOnConfig() checks for the hash:**\n```go\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) DependsOnConfig(config ConfigKey) bool {\n    if sc == nil {\n        return true\n    }\n    ...\n    _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n    return exists  // FALSE if \"reviews-subsets\" was never registered\n}\n```\n\nWhen `reviews-subsets` is updated, DependsOnConfig() is called with:\n```\nConfigKey{Kind: DestinationRule, Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\"}\n```\n\nIts hash is NOT in `configDependencies` because only \"reviews-traffic-policy\" was registered.\n\n---\n\n### 4. xDS Push Filtering (`proxy_dependencies.go:60-74` and `ads.go:688`)\n\n**checkProxyDependencies() calls DependsOnConfig():**\n```go\nfunc checkProxyDependencies(proxy *model.Proxy, config model.ConfigKey) bool {\n    switch proxy.Type {\n    case model.SidecarProxy:\n        if proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {  // Returns FALSE\n            return true\n        } else if proxy.PrevSidecarScope != nil && proxy.PrevSidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false  // Returns FALSE here\n}\n```\n\n**ConfigAffectsProxy() uses checkProxyDependencies():**\n```go\nfunc ConfigAffectsProxy(req *model.PushRequest, proxy *model.Proxy) bool {\n    for config := range req.ConfigsUpdated {\n        if affected && checkProxyDependencies(proxy, config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false  // Returns FALSE\n}\n```\n\n**DefaultProxyNeedsPush() checks ConfigAffectsProxy():**\n```go\nfunc DefaultProxyNeedsPush(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) bool {\n    if ConfigAffectsProxy(req, proxy) {  // Returns FALSE\n        return true\n    }\n    ...\n    return false  // Returns FALSE\n}\n```\n\n**ads.go:688 skips the push:**\n```go\nif !s.ProxyNeedsPush(con.proxy, pushRequest) {\n    log.Debugf(\"Skipping push to %v, no updates required\", con.conID)\n    if pushRequest.Full {\n        reportAllEvents(s.StatusReporter, con.conID, pushRequest.Push.LedgerVersion, nil)\n    }\n    return nil  // PUSH IS SKIPPED\n}\n```\n\nThe proxy receives no updated configuration and continues serving stale Envoy routes and clusters.\n\n---\n\n### 5. Consolidated Structure Hides Multiple DRs (`push_context.go:251-256`)\n\n```go\ntype consolidatedDestRules struct {\n    exportTo map[host.Name]map[visibility.Instance]bool\n    destRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config  // Map of hostname to LIST of configs\n}\n```\n\nWhile the structure supports multiple DRs per hostname (a list), the merging process ensures that:\n- For matching selectors, only ONE config object survives\n- The others' metadata is lost, making them \"invisible\" to dependency tracking\n\n---\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`** - Merges multiple DRs, loses metadata\n2. **`pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`** - Stores merged DRs in index, no tracking of contributing DRs\n3. **`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`** - Registers only merged DR's metadata in configDependencies\n4. **`pilot/pkg/model/config.go`** - {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01R7VY8cyfUuFpqnZ2w9yJhz","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# Investigation Report: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update\n     2→\n     3→## Summary\n     4→\n     5→When multiple DestinationRules (DRs) target the same host, Istio merges them into a single consolidated configuration during PushContext initialization. The merging process **loses the metadata identity (Name/Namespace) of contributing DRs**, causing only one DR's ConfigKey to be registered in the SidecarScope's config dependencies. When a non-primary DR is updated, the xDS push filter uses DependsOnConfig() to check if the proxy is affected, but the check fails because the updated DR's ConfigKey was never registered. As a result, the xDS push is **silently skipped**, and the Envoy sidecar receives no updated configuration until the pod is restarted.\n     6→\n     7→---\n     8→\n     9→## Root Cause\n    10→\n    11→The root cause is the **loss of metadata identity during DestinationRule merging**, combined with **incomplete dependency tracking** and **incorrect xDS push filtering**.\n    12→\n    13→### Mechanism\n    14→\n    15→1. **Metadata Loss During Merge** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n    16→   - The `mergeDestinationRule()` function merges multiple DRs for the same host by:\n    17→     - Finding the existing DR in `p.destRules[hostname]`\n    18→     - Modifying the EXISTING DR's config object in-place (subsets, traffic policies)\n    19→     - If selectors match, setting `addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false` (line 60)\n    20→     - NOT appending the new DR's config to the list (line 102 is skipped when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules == false`)\n    21→   - **Result**: Only the first DR's `config.Config` object survives in `p.destRules[hostname]`. The second (and subsequent) DR's Name/Namespace metadata is **never stored**.\n    22→\n    23→2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:219-227`)\n    24→   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` iterates over `ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s)` results\n    25→   - For each returned DR, it calls:\n    26→     ```go\n    27→     out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n    28→         Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n    29→         Name:      dr.Name,      // Only the MERGED DR's name\n    30→         Namespace: dr.Namespace, // Only the MERGED DR's namespace\n    31→     })\n    32→     ```\n    33→   - Since `ps.destinationRule()` returns only one `config.Config` per hostname (the merged one), only ONE ConfigKey is registered.\n    34→   - **Result**: The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `sc.configDependencies`.\n    35→\n    36→3. **Push Filter Skips Unknown ConfigKeys** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:521-540`)\n    37→   - When a config update occurs, `DependsOnConfig()` checks if the proxy depends on that config:\n    38→     ```go\n    39→     _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n    40→     return exists\n    41→     ```\n    42→   - The HashCode is based on Kind, Name, and Namespace (lines 60-74 in `pilot/pkg/model/config.go`)\n    43→   - If the updated DR's ConfigKey hash is NOT in the map, `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`.\n    44→\n    45→4. **xDS Push Is Skipped** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go:60-74` and `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:688`)\n    46→   - `checkProxyDependencies()` calls `proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config)` (line 64)\n    47→   - If it returns `false`, the push is filtered out\n    48→   - At line 688 of `ads.go`, if `ProxyNeedsPush()` returns `false`, the push to the proxy is **skipped entirely**\n    49→   - The proxy receives no updated xDS configuration and continues serving stale routes/clusters\n    50→\n    51→---\n    52→\n    53→## Evidence\n    54→\n    55→### 1. Merge Function Loses Metadata (`destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n    56→\n    57→**Line 38-60: Merge Detection and Decision**\n    58→```go\n    59→func (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, ...) {\n    60→    rule := destRuleConfig.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    61→    resolvedHost := ResolveShortnameToFQDN(rule.Host, destRuleConfig.Meta)\n    62→    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n    63→        addRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n    64→        for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n    65→            existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    66→            bothWithoutSelector := rule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil && existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil\n    67→            bothWithSelector := existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil\n    68→            selectorsMatch := labels.Instance(existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels()).Equals(rule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n    69→\n    70→            if bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n    71→                addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false  // LINE 60: Don't add new DR\n    72→            }\n    73→```\n    74→\n    75→**Lines 63-93: Merge Data Into Existing Config**\n    76→```go\n    77→            copied := mdr.DeepCopy()  // Deep copy the EXISTING config\n    78→            p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n    79→            mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    80→\n    81→            // Add subsets from new rule to existing rule\n    82→            for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n    83→                if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; The merging process **loses the metadata identity (Name/Namespace) of contributing DRs**, causing only one DR's ConfigKey to be registered in the SidecarScope's config dependencies. When a non-primary DR is updated, the xDS push filter uses DependsOnConfig() to check if the proxy is affected, but the check fails because the updated DR's ConfigKey was never registered. As a result, the xDS push is **silently skipped**, and the Envoy sidecar receives no updated configuration until the pod is restarted.\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause is the **loss of metadata identity during DestinationRule merging**, combined with **incomplete dependency tracking** and **incorrect xDS push filtering**.\n\n### Mechanism\n\n1. **Metadata Loss During Merge** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n   - The `mergeDestinationRule()` function merges multiple DRs for the same host by:\n     - Finding the existing DR in `p.destRules[hostname]`\n     - Modifying the EXISTING DR's config object in-place (subsets, traffic policies)\n     - If selectors match, setting `addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false` (line 60)\n     - NOT appending the new DR's config to the list (line 102 is skipped when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules == false`)\n   - **Result**: Only the first DR's `config.Config` object survives in `p.destRules[hostname]`. The second (and subsequent) DR's Name/Namespace metadata is **never stored**.\n\n2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:219-227`)\n   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` iterates over `ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s)` results\n   - For each returned DR, it calls:\n     ```go\n     out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n         Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n         Name:      dr.Name,      // Only the MERGED DR's name\n         Namespace: dr.Namespace, // Only the MERGED DR's namespace\n     })\n     ```\n   - Since `ps.destinationRule()` returns only one `config.Config` per hostname (the merged one), only ONE ConfigKey is registered.\n   - **Result**: The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `sc.configDependencies`.\n\n3. **Push Filter Skips Unknown ConfigKeys** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:521-540`)\n   - When a config update occurs, `DependsOnConfig()` checks if the proxy depends on that config:\n     ```go\n     _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n     return exists\n     ```\n   - The HashCode is based on Kind, Name, and Namespace (lines 60-74 in `pilot/pkg/model/config.go`)\n   - If the updated DR's ConfigKey hash is NOT in the map, `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`.\n\n4. **xDS Push Is Skipped** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go:60-74` and `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:688`)\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` calls `proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config)` (line 64)\n   - If it returns `false`, the push is filtered out\n   - At line 688 of `ads.go`, if `ProxyNeedsPush()` returns `false`, the push to the proxy is **skipped entirely**\n   - The proxy receives no updated xDS configuration and continues serving stale routes/clusters\n\n---\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1. Merge Function Loses Metadata (`destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n\n**Line 38-60: Merge Detection and Decision**\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, ...) {\n    rule := destRuleConfig.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    resolvedHost := ResolveShortnameToFQDN(rule.Host, destRuleConfig.Meta)\n    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n        addRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n        for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n            existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            bothWithoutSelector := rule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil && existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil\n            bothWithSelector := existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil\n            selectorsMatch := labels.Instance(existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels()).Equals(rule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n\n            if bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n                addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false  // LINE 60: Don't add new DR\n            }\n```\n\n**Lines 63-93: Merge Data Into Existing Config**\n```go\n            copied := mdr.DeepCopy()  // Deep copy the EXISTING config\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n            mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\n            // Add subsets from new rule to existing rule\n            for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n                if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                    mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Add traffic policy if missing\n            if mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n                mergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n            }\n        }\n```\n\n**Lines 101-104: New DR Config Is NOT Added**\n```go\n        if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {  // This is FALSE when merged\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n        }\n        return  // Exit without adding new DR's config","numLines":100,"startLine":1,"totalLines":424}}}
